Nokia 215 Dual SIM Internet-Ready Feature Phone Launched at Rs. Ketan Pratap , 20 February 2015. Share on Facebook Tweet Share Share Email Reddit Comment. Microsoft has launched the affordable Internet-ready Nokia 215 Dual SIM feature phone in India, priced at Rs. The company quietly listed the budget phone on its official online store for India.. Initially launched in January alongside the Nokia 215 , both the phones share common specifications except that the Nokia 215 Dual SIM also features dual-SIM support, as the name suggests. Both the handsets support Micro-SIM cards.. It features a 2.4-inch QVGA (240x320 pixels) LCD display offering a pixel density of 166ppi. The phone supports expandable storage via microSD card (up to 32GB). The Nokia 215 Dual SIM packs an 1100mAh removable battery. The company claims that the battery can deliver up to 21 days of standby time and up to 20 hours of talk time on 2G networks.. ( Also see : Nokia 215 vs Nokia 215 Dual SIM ). It sports a 0.3-megapixel fixed-focus camera and runs on Series 30+ operating system. Connectivity options on the Nokia 215 Dual SIM include Bluetooth 3.0, GPRS, and Micro-USB.. The Nokia 215 Dual SIM comes with Opera Mini Browser and Bing Search pre-installed. The handset packs a built-in torchlight and also includes stereo FM radio. It is currently available in a choice of colours, namely - Bright Green, Black, and White.. Earlier this week, Microsoft silently launched the Lumia 532 Dual SIM in India at Rs. The Microsoft Lumia 435 Dual SIM officially listed last week at Rs. 5,999 was also announced at the same price alongside the Lumia 532 Dual SIM.. Both the Microsoft Lumia 435 Dual SIM and Microsoft Lumia 532 Dual SIM were launched in January alongside single-SIM variants - Microsoft Lumia 435 and Microsoft Lumia 532 .. On Thursday, the company announced 'guaranteed cashback offers' on its high-end Lumia 930 and Lumia 830 smartphones. The Lumia 830 and Lumia 930 will be now available at new prices of Rs. 31,600 respectively after the cashback offer starting Friday.. Wireless transfer of data with Bluetooth enabled devices is possible with the inclusion of built in Bluetooth 3.0. The Microsoft 215 Dual Sim features a 2.4-inch TFT display with a resolution of 240 x 320 pixels and a pixel density of 167ppi. It is packed in a 12.9mm thick outfit which has a weight of just 78g.. The Microsoft 215 Dual Sim packs a 0.3MP camera which supports 2X digital zoom and can shoot QVGA videos at 15fps framerate. It has an internal memory of 8MP which can be expanded up to 32GB via microSD slot.. The Microsoft 215 Dual Sim comes with dual SIM slots and supports GPRS, Bluetooth v3.0 with SLAM and USB port. You can access the web via the Opera Mini browser and stay connected with apps like Twitter, Facebook, Bing and Facebook Messenger. A SIM card or Subscriber Identity Module is a portable memory chip used in GSM phones. The SIM Card allows users to change phones by simply removing the SIM Card from one cell phone and inserting it into another. The SIM holds personal identity information, cell phone number, phone book, text messages and other data. How does the remote unlocking work?. Upon successful order submission, we will process your Nokia 215 Dual SIM Unlock Code's unique IMEI number and email back an unlock code. The International Mobile Equipment Identity or IMEI is a 15 digit serial number unique to every GSM cell phone. We generate the unlocking code from the IMEI, this is called remote unlocking. Equipped with a 2.4inch TFT display, the phone generates 240 x 320 pixel resolution visual performances with ease. The phone features a sizeable internal storage space that can save info of multiple contacts, messages, and much more. A long lasting battery eliminates the need for frequent charging, enabling you to play/work for extended hours.. The Nokia 215 Dual SIM weighs just 78.6g and has dimensions measuring 116 x 50 x 12.9mm. The compact footprint makes it easy to carry the phone even while traveling. The phone sports a 2.4inch TFT color screen that generates 240 x 320 pixel resolution images with 256K color output. These images also feature a pixel density of around 167ppi. The phone features a stylish alphanumeric keypad and a Navi key which eases out the typing and navigation while using the phone.. The Nokia 215 Dual SIM operates on a propriety OS that effectively simplifies the phone’s user interface. The device’s built in 8MB RAM facilitates glitch free multitasking between different open applications.. The phone features a WAP 2.0/xHTML browser, which permits faster loading of web pages and web content. Wireless transfer of data with Bluetooth enabled devices is possible with the inclusion of built in Bluetooth 3.0. The phone also incorporates a microUSB port that facilitates high speed data transfers between this device and your computer.. The Nokia 215 Dual SIM is powered by an 1100mAh Lithium Ion battery that offers a substantial standby and talk time. The phone has a sizeable internal storage space that can store details of up to 1000 different contacts.
